3.6%</li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Language">Language</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Grenada&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Language">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" width="50" height="39" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399" /></a></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>does not <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">cite</a> any <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">sources</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Grenada&amp;action=edit">improve this section</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Burden_of_evidence" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">removed</a>.</span>  <small><i>(March 2018)</i></small><small class="hide-when-compact"><i> (<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p><a href="/wiki/English_language" title="English language">English</a> is the country\'s official language, but the main spoken language is either of two <a href="/wiki/Creole_language" title="Creole language">creole languages</a> (<a href="/wiki/Grenadian_Creole_English" class="mw-redirect" title="Grenadian Creole English">Grenadian Creole English</a> and <a href="/wiki/Grenadian_Creole" title="Grenadian Creole">Grenadian Creole French</a>) which reflects the African, European, and native Indian heritage of the nation. The creoles contain elements from a variety of African languages; Grenadian Creole, however, is also influenced by <a href="/wiki/French_language" title="French language">French</a>.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Grenadian_Creole" title="Grenadian Creole">Grenadian Creole French</a> is mainly spoken in smaller rural areas, but today it can only be heard in a few small pockets of the society. Grenadian Creole French is mainly known as <a href="/wiki/Patois" title="Patois">Patois</a> or <a href="/wiki/French-based_creole_languages" title="French-based creole languages">Creole</a>.\n</p><p>Some <a href="/wiki/Hindi" title="Hindi">Hindi</a>/<a href="/wiki/Bhojpuri" class="mw-redirect" title="Bhojpuri">Bhojpuri</a> terms are still spoken amongst the Indian descendants, mostly those pertaining to the kitchen; such as <i>aloo, geera, karela, seim, chownkay, and baylay.</i> The term <i>bhai</i>, which means "brother" in <a href="/wiki/Urdu" title="Urdu">Urdu</a> and Hindi, is a common form of greeting amongst <a href="/wiki/Indo-Grenadians" title="Indo-Grenadians">Indo-Grenadians</a> males of equal status.\n</p><p>The indigenous languages were <a href="/wiki/I%C3%B1eri_language" class="mw-redirect" title="I\xc3\xb1eri language">I\xc3\xb1eri</a> and <a href="/wiki/Karina_language" class="mw-redirect" title="Karina language">Karina</a> (Carib).\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Culture">Culture</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Grenada&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Culture">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" width="50" height="39" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399" /></a></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>does not <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">cite</a> any <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">sources</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Grenada&amp;action=edit">improve this section</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Burden_of_evidence" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">removed</a>.</span>  <small><i>(March 2018)</i></small><small class="hide-when-compact"><i> (<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Culture_of_Grenada" title="Culture of Grenada">Culture of Grenada</a> and <a href="/wiki/Music_of_Grenada" title="Music of Grenada">Music of Grenada</a></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:GrenadaCarnival1965FeatheredHeaddresses.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/GrenadaCarnival1965FeatheredHeaddresses.jpg/220px-GrenadaCarnival1965FeatheredHeaddresses.jpg" width="220" height="210" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/GrenadaCarnival1965FeatheredHeaddresses.jpg/330px-GrenadaCarnival1965FeatheredHeaddresses.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/GrenadaCarnival1965FeatheredHeaddresses.jpg/440px-GrenadaCarnival1965FeatheredHeaddresses.jpg 2x" data-file-width="903" data-file-height="863" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:GrenadaCarnival1965FeatheredHeaddresses.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>1965 carnival</div></div></div>\n<p>Although French influence on Grenadian culture is much less visible than on other <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_islands" class="mw-redirect" title="Caribbean islands">Caribbean islands</a>, surnames and place names in French remain, and the everyday language is laced with French words and the local dialect, or Patois. Stronger French influence is found in the well seasoned <a href="/wiki/Spice" title="Spice">spicy food</a> and styles of cooking similar to those found in <a href="/wiki/New_Orleans" title="New Orleans">New Orleans</a>, and some French architecture has survived from the 1700s. Island culture is heavily influenced by the <a href="/wiki/Ethnic_groups_of_Africa" class="mw-redirect" title="Ethnic groups of Africa">African</a> roots of most of the Grenadians, but <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">Indian</a> and <a href="/wiki/Island_Caribs" title="Island Caribs">Carib Amerindian</a> influence is also seen with <a href="/wiki/Dal" title="Dal">dhal</a> puri, rotis, Indian sweets, cassava and curries in the cuisine.\n</p><p>The "oildown" is considered to be the national dish. The name refers to a dish cooked in coconut milk until all the milk is absorbed, leaving a bit of coconut oil in the bottom of the pot. Early recipes call for a mixture of salted pigtail, pig\'s feet (trotters), salt beef and chicken, dumplings made from flour, and provision like breadfruit, green banana, yam and potatoes. <a href="/wiki/Callaloo" title="Callaloo">Callaloo</a> leaves are sometimes used to retain the steam and for extra flavour.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Soca_music" title="Soca music">Soca</a>, <a href="/wiki/Calypso_music" title="Calypso music">calypso</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Reggae" title="Reggae">reggae</a> set the mood for Grenada\'s annual <a href="/wiki/Carnival" title="Carnival">Carnival</a> activities. Over the years <a href="/wiki/Rap" class="mw-redirect" title="Rap">rap</a> music became famous among Grenadian youths, and there have been numerous young rappers emerging in the island\'s underground rap scene. <a href="/wiki/Zouk" title="Zouk">Zouk</a> is also being slowly introduced onto the island. The islanders\' African and Carib Amerindian heritage plays an influential role in many aspects of Grenada\'s culture.\n</p><p>An important aspect of the Grenadian culture is the tradition of <a href="/wiki/Storytelling" title="Storytelling">story telling</a>, with <a href="/wiki/Folklore" title="Folklore">folk tales</a> bearing both African and French influences. The character, <i><a href="/wiki/Anansi" title="Anansi">Anancy</a></i>, a spider who is a <a href="/wiki/Trickster" title="Trickster">trickster</a>, originated in <a href="/wiki/West_Africa" title="West Africa">West Africa</a> and is prevalent on other islands as well. French influence can be seen in <i><a href="/wiki/La_Diablesse" title="La Diablesse">La Diablesse</a></i>, a well-dressed she-<a href="/wiki/Devil" title="Devil">devil</a>, and <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ligaroo&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Ligaroo (page does not exist)">Ligaroo</a></i> (from "loup-garou"), a <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a>.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">Sports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Grenada&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Sports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Olympics">Olympics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Grenada&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Olympics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Grenada_at_the_Olympics" title="Grenada at the Olympics">Grenada at the Olympics</a></div>\n<p>Grenada has competed in every Summer Olympics since the <a href="/wiki/1984_Summer_Olympics" title="1984 Summer Olympics">1984 Summer Olympics</a> in Los Angeles.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> <a href="/wiki/Kirani_James" title="Kirani James">Kirani James</a> won the first <a href="/wiki/Olympic_games" class="mw-redirect" title="Olympic games">Olympic</a> <a href="/wiki/Gold_medal" title="Gold medal">gold medal</a> for Grenada in the <a href="/wiki/Athletics_at_the_2012_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_400_metres" title="Athletics at the 2012 Summer Olympics \xe2\x80\x93 Men&#39;s 400 metres">men\'s 400 meters</a> in <a href="/wiki/2012_Summer_Olympics" title="2012 Summer Olympics">2012</a> and silver in <a href="/wiki/2016_Summer_Olympics" title="2016 Summer Olympics">2016</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cricket">Cricket</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Grenada&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Cricket">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cricket_in_the_West_Indies" title="Cricket in the West Indies">Cricket in the West Indies</a> and <a href="/wiki/Windward_Islands_cricket_team" title="Windward Islands cricket team">Windward Islands cricket team</a></div>\n<p>As with other islands from the Caribbean, <a href="/wiki/Cricket" title="Cricket">cricket</a> is the national and most popular sport and is an intrinsic part of Grenadian culture.  The <a href="/wiki/Grenada_national_cricket_team" title="Grenada national cricket team">Grenada national cricket team</a> forms a part of the <a href="/wiki/Windward_Islands_cricket_team" title="Windward Islands cricket team">Windward Islands cricket team</a> in regional domestic cricket, however it plays as a separate entity in minor regional matches,<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> as well as having previously played <a href="/wiki/Twenty20" title="Twenty20">Twenty20</a> cricket in the <a href="/wiki/Stanford_20/20" title="Stanford 20/20">Stanford 20/20</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Grenada_National_Cricket_Stadium" class="mw-redirect" title="Grenada National Cricket Stadium">Grenada National Cricket Stadium</a> of <a href="/wiki/St._George%27s,_Grenada" title="St. George&#39;s, Grenada">St. George\'s</a> hosts domestic and international cricket matches. <a href="/wiki/Devon_Smith" title="Devon Smith">Devon Smith</a>, West Indies record holder to win the <a href="/wiki/List-A_cricket" class="mw-redirect" title="List-A cricket">List-A</a> West Indian <a href="/wiki/WICB_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="WICB Cup">domestic competition</a> for the second time, was born in the small town of <a href="/wiki/Hermitage_(Carriacou)" title="Hermitage (Carriacou)">Hermitage</a>.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Grenada&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: See also">edit</a><span
